\"adding dependency would create a cycle\",\n    95→            DependencyGraphError.IssueNotFound => \"issue not found\",\n    96→            else => \"failed to add dependency\",\n    97→        };\n    98→        try outputError(&ctx.output, structured_output, msg);\n    99→\n   100→        return switch (err) {\n   101→            DependencyGraphError.SelfDependency =>         else => DepError.StorageError,\n   105→        };\n   106→    };\n   107→\n   108→    try ctx.saveIfAutoFlush();\n   109→\n   110→    if (structured_output) {\n   111→        try 200→            for (deps) |dep| {\n   201→                try output.print(\"  - {s} ({s})\\n\", .{ dep.depends_on_id, dep.dep_type.toString() });\n   202→            }\n   203→        } else {\n 221→    title: []const u8,\n   222→    status: []const u8,\n   223→    children: ?[]const TreeNode = null,\n   224→};\n   225→\n   226→fn runTree(\n   227→    graph: *DependencyGraph,\n   228→    ctx: *CommandContext,\n   229→    tree_args: anytype,\n   230→    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n   231→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   232→) !void {\n   233→    const id = tree_args.id;\n   234→\n   235→    // Check if issue exists\n   236→    const issue = try ctx.store.get(id);\n   237→    if (issue == null) {\n   238→        try common.outputNotFoundError(DepResult, &ctx.output, global.isStructuredOutput(), id, allocator);\n   239→        return DepError.IssueNotFound;\n   240→    }\n   241→    var i = issue.?;\n   242→    defer i.deinit(allocator);\n   243→\n   244→    if 254→        // ASCII tree output\n   255→        try ctx.output.println(\"{s} - {s} [{s}]\", .{ id, i.title, i.status.toString() });\n   256→\n   257→        // Show what this issue depends on (upstream dependencies)\n   258→        const deps = try graph.getDependencies(id);\n   259→        defer graph.freeDependencies(deps);\n   260→\n   261→        if (deps.len > 0) {\n   262→ visited.keyIterator();\n   266→                while (it.next()) |key| allocator.free(key.*);\n   267→                visited.deinit(allocator);\n   268→            }\n   269→\n   270→            for (deps, 0..) |dep, idx| {\n   271→                const is_last = (idx == deps.len - 1);\n   272→                try printTreeBranch(&ctx.output, graph, ctx, dep.depends_on_id, \"\", is_last, &visited, graph.getDependents(id);\n   278→        defer graph.freeDependencies(dependents);\n   279→\n   280→        if (dependents.len > 0) {\n   281→            try ctx.output.print(\"\\n\", .{});\n   282→            try ctx.output.println(\"Blocked by this:\", .{});\n   283→            for (dependents, 0..) |dep, idx| {\n   284→                const is_last = (idx == dependents.len - 1);\n   285→                const prefix = if (is_last) \"`-- \" else \"|-- \";\n   286→                const dep_issue = try ctx.store.get(dep.issue_id);\n   287→                if (dep_issue) |di| {\n   288→                    var d = di;\n   289→                    defer d.deinit(allocator);\n   290→                    try ctx.output.print(\"{s}{s} - {s} [{s}]\\n\", .{ prefix, dep.issue_id, d.title, d.status.toString() });\n   291→                } else {\n   292→                    try ctx.output.print(\"{s}{s} (not found)\\n\", .{ prefix, dep.issue_id });\n   293→                }\n   294→            }\n   295→        }\n   296→    }\n   297→}\n   298→\n   299→fn printTreeBranch(\n   300→    output: *common.Output,\n   301→    graph: *DependencyGraph,\n   302→    ctx: *CommandContext,\n   303→    id: []const u8,\n   304→    prefix: []const u8,\n   305→    is_last: bool,\n   306→    visited: *std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(void),\n   307→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   308→    depth: usize,\n   309→    max_depth: usize,\n   310→) !void {\n   311→    // Check for cycles\n   312→    if (visited.contains(id)) {\n   313→        const branch = if (is_last) \"`-- \" else \"|-- \";\n   314→        try output.print(\"{s}{s}{s} (cycle)\\n\", .{ prefix, branch, id });\n   315→        return;\n   316→    }\n   317→\n   318→    // Depth limit\n   319→    if (depth >= max_depth) {\n   320→        const branch = if (is_last) \"`-- \" else \"|-- \";\n   321→        try output.print(\"{s}{s}{s} (...)\\n\", .{ prefix, branch, id });\n   322→        return;\n   323→    }\n   324→\n   325→    // Mark as visited\n   326→    const id_copy = try allocator.dupe(u8, id);\n   327→    errdefer allocator.free(id_copy);\n   328→    try visited.put(allocator, id_copy, {});\n   329→\n   330→    // Get issue details\n   331→    const issue = try ctx.store.get(id);\n   332→    const branch = if (is_last) \"`-- \" else \"|-- \";\n   333→\n   334→    if (issue) |i| {\n   335→        var iss = i;\n   336→        defer iss.deinit(allocator);\n   337→        try output.print(\"{s}{s}{s} - {s} [{s}]\\n\", .{ prefix, branch, id, iss.title, iss.status.toString() });\n   338→    } else {\n   339→        try output.print(\"{s}{s}{s} (not found)\\n\", .{ prefix, branch, id });\n   340→        return;\n   341→    }\n   342→\n   343→    // Get dependencies of this issue\n   344→    const deps = try graph.getDependencies(id);\n   345→    defer graph.freeDependencies(deps);\n   346→\n   347→    // Build new prefix for children\n   348→    var new_prefix_buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n   349→    const extension = if (is_last) \"    \" else \"|   \";\n   350→    const new_prefix = std.fmt.bufPrint(&new_prefix_buf, \"{s}{s}\", .{ prefix, extension }) catch prefix;\n   351→\n   352→    for (deps, 0..) |dep, idx| {\n   353→        const child_is_last = (idx == deps.len - 1);\n   354→        try printTreeBranch(output, graph, ctx, dep.depends_on_id, new_prefix, child_is_last, visited, allocator, depth + 1, max_depth);\n   355→    }\n   356→}\n   357→\n   358→fn buildTreeNode(\n   359→    graph: *DependencyGraph,\n   360→    ctx: *CommandContext,\n   361→    id: []const u8,\n   362→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   363→    depth: usize,\n   364→    max_depth: usize,\n   365→) !TreeNode {\n   366→    const issue = try ctx.store.get(id);\n   367→    var title: []const u8 = \"(not found)\";\n   368→    var status: []const u8 = \"unknown\";\n   369→\n   370→    if (issue) |i| {\n   371→        var iss = i;\n   372→        defer iss.deinit(allocator);\n   373→        title = try allocator.dupe(u8, iss.title);\n   374→        status = iss.status.toString();\n   375→    }\n   376→\n   377→    if (depth >= max_depth) {\n   378→        return TreeNode{\n   379→            .id = try allocator.dupe(u8, id),\n   380→            .title = title,\n   381→            .status = try allocator.dupe(u8, status),\n   382→            .children = null,\n   383→        };\n   384→    }\n   385→\n   386→    const deps = try graph.getDependencies(id);\n   387→    defer graph.freeDependencies(deps);\n   388→\n   389→    var children: ?[]TreeNode = null;\n   390→    if (deps.len > 0) Dependency management commands for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! `bz dep add <child> <parent> [--type blocks]` - Add dependency (child depends on parent)\n//! `bz dep remove <child> <parent>` - Remove dependency\n//! `bz dep list <id>` - List dependencies for an issue\n//!\n//! Manages relationships between issues.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst models = @import(\"../models/mod.zig\");\nconst storage = @import(\"../storage/mod.zig\");\nconst common = *DependencyGraph,\n    ctx: *CommandContext,\n    add_args: anytype,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    const structured_output = global.isStructuredOutput();\n    if (!try ctx.store.exists(add_args.child)) {\n        try common.outputNotFoundError(DepResult, &ctx.output, structured_output, add_args.child, allocator);\n        return DepError.IssueNotFound;\n    }\n\n    if (!try ctx.store.exists(add_args.parent)) {\n        try common.outputNotFoundError(DepResult, &ctx.output, structured_output, add_args.parent, allocator);\n        return DepError.IssueNotFound;\n    }\n\n    const now = std.time.timestamp();\n    const dep = Dependency{\n        .issue_id = add_args.child,\n        .depends_on_id = add_args.parent,\n        .dep_type = DependencyType.fromString(add_args.dep_type),\n        .created_at = now,\n        .created_by = global.actor,\n        .metadata = null,\n        .thread_id = null,\n    };\n\n    graph.addDependency(dep) catch |err| {\n        const msg = switch (err) {\n            DependencyGraphError.SelfDependency => \"cannot depend on self\",\n            DependencyGraphError.CycleDetected => \"adding dependency would create a cycle\",\n            DependencyGraphError.IssueNotFound => \"issue not found\",\n            else => \"failed to add dependency\",\n        };\n        try outputError(&ctx.output, structured_output, msg);\n\n        return switch (err) {\n            DependencyGraphError.SelfDependency => DepError.SelfDependency,\n            DependencyGraphError.CycleDetected => DepError.CycleDetected,\n            DependencyGraphError.IssueNotFound => DepError.IssueNotFound,\n            else => DepError.StorageError,\n        };\n    };\n\n    try ctx.saveIfAutoFlush();\n\n    if (structured_output) {\n        try ctx.output.printJson(DepResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .action = \"added\",\n            .child = add_args.child,\n            .parent = add_args.parent,\n        });\n    } else if (!global.quiet) {\n        try ctx.output.success(\"Added dependency: {s} depends on {s}\", .{ add_args.child, add_args.parent });\n    }\n}\n\nfn runRemove(\n    graph: *DependencyGraph,\n    ctx: *CommandContext,\n    remove_args: anytype,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n) !void {\n ctx: *CommandContext,\n    tree_args: anytype,\n    global: args.GlobalOptions,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n) !void {\n    const id = tree_args.id;\n\n    // Check if issue exists\n    const {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01BmfoySXCKe7sU6kitRPibJ","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→//! Write-Ahead Log (WAL) for beads_zig.\n     2→//!\n     3→//! Provides constant-time concurrent writes by appending operations to a WAL file\n     4→//! rather than rewriting the entire main JSONL file. Operations are:\n     5→//! - Serialized via flock before append\n     6→//! - fsync'd before lock release for durability\n     7→//! - Replayed on read to reconstruct current state\n     8→//!\n     9→//! WAL entry format (JSON lines):\n    10→//! {\"op\":\"add\",\"ts\":1706540000,\"id\":\"bd-abc123\",\"data\":{...}}\n    11→//! {\"op\":\"close\",\"ts\":1706540001,\"id\":\"bd-abc123\",\"data\":null}\n    12→\n    13→const std = @import(\"std\");\n    14→const fs = std.fs;\n    15→const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n    16→const BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\n    17→const IssueStore = @import(\"store.zig\").IssueStore;\n    18→const test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n    19→\n    20→pub const WalError = error{\n    21→    WalCorrupted,\n    22→    WriteError,\n    23→    LockFailed,\n    24→    InvalidOperation,\n    25→    ParseError,\n    26→    OutOfMemory,\n    27→    ReplayPartialFailure,\n    28→};\n    29→\n    30→/// Statistics from WAL replay operations.\n    31→pub const ReplayStats = struct {\n    32→    applied: usize = 0,\n    33→    skipped: usize = 0,\n    34→    failed: usize = 0,\n    35→    failure_ids: []const []const u8 = &.{},\n    36→\n    37→    pub fn deinit(self: *ReplayStats, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n    38→        for (self.failure_ids) |id| {\n    39→            allocator.free(id);\n    40→        }\n    41→        if (self.failure_ids.len > 0) {\n    42→            allocator.free(self.failure_ids);\n    43→        }\n    44→    }\n    45→\n    46→    pub fn hasFailures(self: ReplayStats) bool {\n    47→        return self.failed > 0;\n    48→    }\n    49→};\n    50→\n    51→/// WAL operation types.\n    52→pub const WalOp = enum {\n    53→    add,\n    54→    update,\n    55→    close,\n    56→    reopen,\n    57→    delete,\n    58→    set_blocked,\n    59→    unset_blocked,\n    60→\n    61→    pub fn toString(self: WalOp) []const u8 {\n    62→        return switch (self) {\n    63→            .add => \"add\",\n    64→            .update => \"update\",\n    65→            .close => \"close\",\n    66→            .reopen => \"reopen\",\n    67→            .delete => \"delete\",\n    68→            .set_blocked => \"set_blocked\",\n    69→            .unset_blocked => \"unset_blocked\",\n    70→        };\n    71→    }\n    72→\n    73→    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?WalOp {\n    74→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"add\")) return .add;\n    75→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"update\")) return .update;\n    76→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"close\")) return .close;\n    77→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"reopen\")) return .reopen;\n    78→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"delete\")) return .delete;\n    79→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"set_blocked\")) return .set_blocked;\n    80→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"unset_blocked\")) return .unset_blocked;\n    81→        return null;\n    82→    }\n    83→};\n    84→\n    85→/// A single WAL entry representing one operation.\n    86→pub const WalEntry = struct {\n    87→    op: WalOp,\n    88→    ts: i64, // Unix timestamp for ordering\n    89→    id: []const u8, // Issue ID\n    90→    data: ?Issue, // Full issue for add/update, null for status-only ops\n    91→\n    92→    const Self = @This();\n    93→\n    94→    /// Custom JSON serialization for WalEntry.\n    95→    pub fn jsonStringify(self: Self, jws: anytype) !void {\n    96→        try jws.beginObject();\n    97→\n    98→        try jws.objectField(\"op\");\n    99→        try jws.write(self.op.toString());\n   100→\n   101→        try jws.objectField(\"ts\");\n   102→        try jws.write(self.ts);\n   103→\n   104→        try jws.objectField(\"id\");\n   105→        try jws.write(self.id);\n   106→\n   107→        try jws.objectField(\"data\");\n   108→        if (self.data) |issue| {\n   109→            try jws.write(issue);\n   110→        } else {\n   111→            try jws.write(null);\n   112→        }\n   113→\n   114→        try jws.endObject();\n   115→    }\n   116→};\n   117→\n   118→/// Parsed WAL entry for replay.\n   119→pub const ParsedWalEntry = struct {\n   120→    op: WalOp,\n   121→    ts: i64,\n   122→    id: []const u8,\n   123→    data: ?Issue,\n   124→\n   125→    pub fn deinit(self: *ParsedWalEntry, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n   126→        allocator.free(self.id);\n   127→        if (self.data) |*issue| {\n   128→            var i = issue.*;\n   129→            i.deinit(allocator);\n   130→        }\n   131→    }\n   132→};\n   133→\n   134→/// WAL file manager for reading and writing operations.\n   135→pub const Wal = struct {\n   136→    wal_path: []const u8,\n   137→    lock_path: []const u8,\n   138→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   139→\n   140→    const Self = @This();\n   141→\n   142→    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Self {\n   143→        const wal_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"beads.wal\" });\n   144→        errdefer allocator.free(wal_path);\n   145→\n   146→        const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n   147→\n   148→        return Self{\n   149→            .wal_path = wal_path,\n   150→            .lock_path = lock_path,\n   151→            .allocator = allocator,\n   152→        };\n   153→    }\n   154→\n   155→    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n   156→        self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n   157→        self.allocator.free(self.lock_path);\n   158→    }\n   159→\n   160→    /// Append an entry to the WAL under exclusive lock.\n   161→    /// Ensures durability via fsync before releasing lock.\n   162→    pub fn appendEntry(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n   163→        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(self.lock_path) catch return WalError.LockFailed;\n   164→        defer lock.release();\n   165→\n   166→        try self.appendEntryUnlocked(entry);\n   167→    }\n   168→\n   169→    /// Append entry without acquiring lock (caller must hold lock).\n   170→    fn appendEntryUnlocked(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n   171→        const dir = fs.cwd();\n   172→\n   173→        // Ensure parent directory exists\n   174→        if (std.fs.path.dirname(self.wal_path)) |parent| {\n   175→            dir.makePath(parent) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   176→                error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n   177→                else => return err,\n   178→            };\n   179→        }\n   180→\n   181→        // Open or create WAL file in append mode\n   182→        const file = dir.createFile(self.wal_path, .{\n   183→            .truncate = false,\n   184→        }) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   185→        defer file.close();\n   186→\n   187→        // Seek to end\n   188→        file.seekFromEnd(0) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   189→\n   190→        // Serialize entry\n   191→        const json_bytes = std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, entry, .{}) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   192→        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n   193→\n   194→        // Write entry + newline\n   195→        file.writeAll(json_bytes) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   196→        file.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   197→\n   198→        // fsync for durability\n   199→        file.sync() catch return WalError.WriteError;\n   200→    }\n   201→\n   202→    /// Read all WAL entries.\n   203→    pub fn readEntries(self: *Self) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n   204→        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(self.wal_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   205→            error.FileNotFound => return &[_]ParsedWalEntry{},\n   206→            else => return err,\n   207→        };\n   208→        defer file.close();\n   209→\n   210→        const content = file.readToEndAlloc(self.allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n   211→        defer self.allocator.free(content);\n   212→\n   213→        var entries: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(ParsedWalEntry) = .{};\n   214→        errdefer {\n   215→            for (entries.items) |*e| {\n   216→                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n   217→            }\n   218→            entries.deinit(self.allocator);\n   219→        }\n   220→\n   221→        var line_start: usize = 0;\n   222→        for (content, 0..) |c, i| {\n   223→            if (c == '\\n') {\n   224→                const line = content[line_start..i];\n   225→                line_start = i + 1;\n   226→\n   227→                if (line.len == 0) continue;\n   228→\n   229→                if (self.parseEntry(line)) |entry| {\n   230→                    try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n   231→                } else |_| {\n   232→                    // Skip malformed entries (graceful degradation)\n   233→                    continue;\n   234→                }\n   235→            }\n   236→        }\n   237→\n   238→        // Handle last line if no trailing newline\n   239→        if (line_start < content.len) {\n   240→            const line = content[line_start..];\n   241→            if (line.len > 0) {\n   242→                if (self.parseEntry(line)) |entry| {\n   243→                    try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n   244→                } else |_| {}\n   245→            }\n   246→        }\n   247→\n   248→        return entries.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n   249→    }\n   250→\n   251→    /// Parse a single WAL entry line.\n   252→    fn parseEntry(self: *Self, line: []const u8) !ParsedWalEntry {\n   253→        const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n   254→            struct {\n   255→                op: []const u8,\n   256→                ts: i64,\n   257→                id: []const u8,\n   258→                data: ?Issue,\n   259→            },\n   260→            self.allocator,\n   261→            line,\n   262→            .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n   263→        ) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n   264→        defer parsed.deinit();\n   265→\n   266→        const op = WalOp.fromString(parsed.value.op) orelse return WalError.InvalidOperation;\n   267→\n   268→        // Clone strings since parsed will be freed\n   269→        const id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, parsed.value.id);\n   270→        errdefer self.allocator.free(id);\n   271→\n   272→        var data: ?Issue = null;\n   273→        if (parsed.value.data) |issue| {\n   274→            data = try issue.clone(self.allocator);\n   275→        }\n   276→\n   277→        return ParsedWalEntry{\n   278→            .op = op,\n   279→            .ts = parsed.value.ts,\n   280→            .id = id,\n   281→            .data = data,\n   282→        };\n   283→    }\n   284→\n   285→    /// Replay WAL entries onto an IssueStore.\n   286→    /// Applies operations in timestamp order.\n   287→    /// Returns statistics about the replay including any failures.\n   288→    pub fn replay(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore) !ReplayStats {\n   289→        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n   290→        defer {\n   291→            for (entries) |*e| {\n   292→                var entry = e.*;\n   293→                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n   294→            }\n   295→            self.allocator.free(entries);\n   296→        }\n   297→\n   298→        // Sort by timestamp (sortUnstable mutates through the slice pointer)\n   299→        std.mem.sortUnstable(ParsedWalEntry, @constCast(entries), {}, struct {\n   300→            fn lessThan(_: void, a: ParsedWalEntry, b: ParsedWalEntry) bool {\n   301→                return a.ts < b.ts;\n   302→            }\n   303→        }.lessThan);\n   304→\n   305→        // Track replay results\n   306→        var stats = ReplayStats{};\n   307→        var failure_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n   308→        errdefer {\n   309→            for (failure_ids.items) |id| {\n   310→                self.allocator.free(id);\n   311→            }\n   312→            failure_ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n   313→        }\n   314→\n   315→        // Apply each operation\n   316→        for (entries) |entry| {\n   317→            const result = self.applyEntry(store, entry);\n   318→            switch (result) {\n   319→                .applied => stats.applied += 1,\n   320→                .skipped => stats.skipped += 1,\n   321→                .failed => {\n   322→                    stats.failed += 1;\n   323→                    const id_copy = self.allocator.dupe(u8, entry.id) catch continue;\n   324→                    failure_ids.append(self.allocator, id_copy) catch {\n   325→                        self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n   326→                    };\n   327→                },\n   328→            }\n   329→        }\n   330→\n   331→        stats.failure_ids = failure_ids.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch &.{};\n   332→        return stats;\n   333→    }\n   334→\n   335→    /// Result of applying a single WAL entry.\n   336→    const ApplyResult = enum {\n   337→        applied,\n   338→        skipped,\n   339→        failed,\n   340→    };\n   341→\n   342→    /// Apply a single WAL entry to the store.\n   343→    /// Returns the result of the operation.\n   344→    fn applyEntry(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore, entry: ParsedWalEntry) ApplyResult {\n   345→        _ = self;\n   346→        switch (entry.op) {\n   347→            .add => {\n   348→                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n   349→                    // Only insert if not already present\n   350→                    if (!store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n   351→                        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   352→                            error.DuplicateId => return .skipped, // Already exists\n   353→                            else => return .failed,\n   354→                        };\n   355→                        return .applied;\n   356→                    }\n   357→                    return .skipped; // Already exists\n   358→                }\n   359→                return .skipped; // No data for add op\n   360→            },\n   361→            .update => {\n   362→                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n   363→                    // Update or insert\n   364→                    if (store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n   365→                        // Full replacement for simplicity\n   366→                        const idx = store.id_index.get(issue.id).?;\n   367→                        var old = &store.issues.items[idx];\n   368→                        old.deinit(store.allocator);\n   369→                        store.issues.items[idx] = issue.clone(store.allocator) catch return .failed;\n   370→                        return .applied;\n   371→                    } else {\n   372→                        store.insert(issue) catch return .failed;\n   373→                        return .applied;\n   374→                    }\n   375→                }\n   376→                return .skipped; // No data for update op\n   377→            },\n   378→            .close => {\n   379→                store.update(entry.id, .{\n   380→                    .status = .closed,\n   381→                    .closed_at = std.time.timestamp(),\n   382→                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   383→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   384→                    else => return .failed,\n   385→                };\n   386→                return .applied;\n   387→            },\n   388→            .reopen => {\n   389→                store.update(entry.id, .{\n   390→                    .status = .open,\n   391→                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   392→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   393→                    else => return .failed,\n   394→                };\n   395→                return .applied;\n   396→            },\n   397→            .delete => {\n   398→                store.delete(entry.id, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   399→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   400→                    else => return .failed,\n   401→                };\n   402→                return .applied;\n   403→            },\n   404→            .set_blocked => {\n   405→                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .blocked }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   406→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   407→                    else => return .failed,\n   408→                };\n   409→                return .applied;\n   410→            },\n   411→            .unset_blocked => {\n   412→                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .open }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   413→                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n   414→                    else => return .failed,\n   415→                };\n   416→                return .applied;\n   417→            },\n   418→        }\n   419→    }\n   420→\n   421→    /// Get the number of entries in the WAL.\n   422→    pub fn entryCount(self: *Self) !usize {\n   423→        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n   424→        defer {\n   425→            for (entries) |*e| {\n   426→                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n   427→            }\n   428→            self.allocator.free(entries);\n   429→        }\n   430→        return entries.len;\n   431→    }\n   432→\n   433→    /// Get the size of the WAL file in bytes.\n   434→    pub fn fileSize(self: *Self) !u64 {\n   435→        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(self.wal_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   436→            error.FileNotFound => return 0,\n   437→            else => return err,\n   438→        };\n   439→        defer file.close();\n   440→\n   441→        const stat = try file.stat();\n   442→        return stat.size;\n   443→    }\n   444→\n   445→    /// Truncate the WAL file (used after compaction).\n   446→    pub fn truncate(self: *Self) !void {\n   447→        const dir = fs.cwd();\n   448→        dir.deleteFile(self.wal_path) catch |err| switch (err) {\n   449→            error.FileNotFound => {}, // Already empty\n   450→            else => return err,\n   451→        };\n   452→    }\n   453→\n   454→    // Convenience methods for common operations\n   455→\n   456→    /// Add a new issue to the WAL.\n   457→    pub fn addIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   458→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   459→            .op = .add,\n   460→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   461→            .id = issue.id,\n   462→            .data = issue,\n   463→        });\n   464→    }\n   465→\n   466→    /// Close an issue in the WAL.\n   467→    pub fn closeIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   468→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   469→            .op = .close,\n   470→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   471→            .id = id,\n   472→            .data = null,\n   473→        });\n   474→    }\n   475→\n   476→    /// Reopen an issue in the WAL.\n   477→    pub fn reopenIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   478→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   479→            .op = .reopen,\n   480→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   481→            .id = id,\n   482→            .data = null,\n   483→        });\n   484→    }\n   485→\n   486→    /// Update an issue in the WAL.\n   487→    pub fn updateIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   488→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   489→            .op = .update,\n   490→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   491→            .id = issue.id,\n   492→            .data = issue,\n   493→        });\n   494→    }\n   495→\n   496→    /// Delete an issue in the WAL (tombstone).\n   497→    pub fn deleteIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   498→        try self.appendEntry(.{\n   499→            .op = .delete,\n   500→            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n   501→            .id = id,\n   502→            .data = null,\n   503→        });\n   504→    }\n   505→\n   506→    /// Set an issue as blocked in the WAL.\n   507→    pub fn 523→        });\n   524→    }\n   525→};\n   526→\n   527→// --- Tests ---\n   528→\n   529→test \"WalOp.toString and fromString roundtrip\" {\n   530→    const ops = [_]WalOp{ .add, .update, .close, Write-Ahead Log (WAL) for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Provides constant-time concurrent writes by appending operations to a WAL file\n//! rather than rewriting the entire main JSONL file. Operations are:\n//! - Serialized via flock before append\n//! - fsync'd before lock release for durability\n//! - Replayed on read to reconstruct current state\n//!\n//! WAL entry format (JSON lines):\n//! {\"op\":\"add\",\"ts\":1706540000,\"id\":\"bd-abc123\",\"data\":{...}}\n//! {\"op\":\"close\",\"ts\":1706540001,\"id\":\"bd-abc123\",\"data\":null}\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst fs = std.fs;\nconst Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\nconst BeadsLock = @import(\"lock.zig\").BeadsLock;\nconst IssueStore = @import(\"store.zig\").IssueStore;\nconst test_util = @import(\"../test_util.zig\");\n\npub const WalError = error{\n    WalCorrupted,\n    WriteError,\n    LockFailed,\n    InvalidOperation,\n    ParseError,\n    OutOfMemory,\n    ReplayPartialFailure,\n};\n\n/// Statistics from WAL replay operations.\npub const ReplayStats = struct {\n    applied: usize = 0,\n    skipped: usize = 0,\n    failed: usize = 0,\n    failure_ids: []const []const u8 = &.{},\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *ReplayStats, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n        for (self.failure_ids) |id| {\n            allocator.free(id);\n        }\n        if (self.failure_ids.len > 0) {\n            allocator.free(self.failure_ids);\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn hasFailures(self: ReplayStats) bool {\n        return self.failed > 0;\n    }\n};\n\n/// WAL operation types.\npub const WalOp = enum {\n    add,\n    update,\n    close,\n    reopen,\n    delete,\n    set_blocked,\n    unset_blocked,\n\n    pub fn toString(self: WalOp) []const u8 {\n        return switch (self) {\n            .add => \"add\",\n            .update => \"update\",\n            .close => \"close\",\n            .reopen => \"reopen\",\n            .delete => \"delete\",\n            .set_blocked => \"set_blocked\",\n            .unset_blocked => \"unset_blocked\",\n        };\n    }\n\n    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?WalOp {\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"add\")) return .add;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"update\")) return .update;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"close\")) return .close;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"reopen\")) return .reopen;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"delete\")) return .delete;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"set_blocked\")) return .set_blocked;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, s, \"unset_blocked\")) return .unset_blocked;\n        return null;\n    }\n};\n\n/// A single WAL entry representing one operation.\npub const WalEntry = struct {\n    op: WalOp,\n    ts: i64, // Unix timestamp for ordering\n    id: []const u8, // Issue ID\n    data: ?Issue, // Full issue for add/update, null for status-only ops\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    /// Custom JSON serialization for WalEntry.\n    pub fn jsonStringify(self: Self, jws: anytype) !void {\n        try jws.beginObject();\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"op\");\n        try jws.write(self.op.toString());\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"ts\");\n        try jws.write(self.ts);\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"id\");\n        try jws.write(self.id);\n\n        try jws.objectField(\"data\");\n        if (self.data) |issue| {\n            try jws.write(issue);\n        } else {\n            try jws.write(null);\n        }\n\n        try jws.endObject();\n    }\n};\n\n/// Parsed WAL entry for replay.\npub const ParsedWalEntry = struct {\n    op: WalOp,\n    ts: i64,\n    id: []const u8,\n    data: ?Issue,\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *ParsedWalEntry, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n        allocator.free(self.id);\n        if (self.data) |*issue| {\n            var i = issue.*;\n            i.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// WAL file manager for reading and writing operations.\npub const Wal = struct {\n    wal_path: []const u8,\n    lock_path: []const u8,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Self {\n        const wal_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"beads.wal\" });\n        errdefer allocator.free(wal_path);\n\n        const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ beads_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n\n        return Self{\n            .wal_path = wal_path,\n            .lock_path = lock_path,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n        };\n    }\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n        self.allocator.free(self.wal_path);\n        self.allocator.free(self.lock_path);\n    }\n\n    /// Append an entry to the WAL under exclusive lock.\n    /// Ensures durability via fsync before releasing lock.\n    pub fn appendEntry(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(self.lock_path) catch return WalError.LockFailed;\n        defer lock.release();\n\n        try self.appendEntryUnlocked(entry);\n    }\n\n    /// Append entry without acquiring lock (caller must hold lock).\n    fn appendEntryUnlocked(self: *Self, entry: WalEntry) !void {\n        const dir = fs.cwd();\n\n        // Ensure parent directory exists\n        if (std.fs.path.dirname(self.wal_path)) |parent| {\n            dir.makePath(parent) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                error.PathAlreadyExists => {},\n                else => return err,\n            };\n        }\n\n        // Open or create WAL file in append mode\n        const file = dir.createFile(self.wal_path, .{\n            .truncate = false,\n        }) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n        defer file.close();\n\n        // Seek to end\n        file.seekFromEnd(0) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n\n        // Serialize entry\n        const json_bytes = std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, entry, .{}) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n        defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n\n        // Write entry + newline\n        file.writeAll(json_bytes) catch return WalError.WriteError;\n        file.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch return WalError.WriteError;\n\n        // fsync for durability\n        file.sync() catch return WalError.WriteError;\n    }\n\n    /// Read all WAL entries.\n    pub fn readEntries(self: *Self) ![]ParsedWalEntry {\n        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(self.wal_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => return &[_]ParsedWalEntry{},\n            else => return err,\n        };\n        defer file.close();\n\n        const content = file.readToEndAlloc(self.allocator, 100 * 1024 * 1024) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n        defer self.allocator.free(content);\n\n        var entries: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(ParsedWalEntry) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (entries.items) |*e| {\n                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            entries.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        var line_start: usize = 0;\n        for (content, 0..) |c, i| {\n            if (c == '\\n') {\n                const line = content[line_start..i];\n                line_start = i + 1;\n\n                if (line.len == 0) continue;\n\n                if (self.parseEntry(line)) |entry| {\n                    try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n                } else |_| {\n                    // Skip malformed entries (graceful degradation)\n                    continue;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Handle last line if no trailing newline\n        if (line_start < content.len) {\n            const line = content[line_start..];\n            if (line.len > 0) {\n                if (self.parseEntry(line)) |entry| {\n                    try entries.append(self.allocator, entry);\n                } else |_| {}\n            }\n        }\n\n        return entries.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a single WAL entry line.\n    fn parseEntry(self: *Self, line: []const u8) !ParsedWalEntry {\n        const parsed = std.json.parseFromSlice(\n            struct {\n                op: []const u8,\n                ts: i64,\n                id: []const u8,\n                data: ?Issue,\n            },\n            self.allocator,\n            line,\n            .{ .ignore_unknown_fields = true, .allocate = .alloc_always },\n        ) catch return WalError.ParseError;\n        defer parsed.deinit();\n\n        const op = WalOp.fromString(parsed.value.op) orelse return WalError.InvalidOperation;\n\n        // Clone strings since parsed will be freed\n        const id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, parsed.value.id);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(id);\n\n        var data: ?Issue = null;\n        if (parsed.value.data) |issue| {\n            data = try issue.clone(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        return ParsedWalEntry{\n            .op = op,\n            .ts = parsed.value.ts,\n            .id = id,\n            .data = data,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Replay WAL entries onto an IssueStore.\n    /// Applies operations in timestamp order.\n    /// Returns statistics about the replay including any failures.\n    pub fn replay(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore) !ReplayStats {\n        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n        defer {\n            for (entries) |*e| {\n                var entry = e.*;\n                entry.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            self.allocator.free(entries);\n        }\n\n        // Sort by timestamp (sortUnstable mutates through the slice pointer)\n        std.mem.sortUnstable(ParsedWalEntry, @constCast(entries), {}, struct {\n            fn lessThan(_: void, a: ParsedWalEntry, b: ParsedWalEntry) bool {\n                return a.ts < b.ts;\n            }\n        }.lessThan);\n\n        // Track replay results\n        var stats = ReplayStats{};\n        var failure_ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (failure_ids.items) |id| {\n                self.allocator.free(id);\n            }\n            failure_ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        // Apply each operation\n        for (entries) |entry| {\n            const result = self.applyEntry(store, entry);\n            switch (result) {\n                .applied => stats.applied += 1,\n                .skipped => stats.skipped += 1,\n                .failed => {\n                    stats.failed += 1;\n                    const id_copy = self.allocator.dupe(u8, entry.id) catch continue;\n                    failure_ids.append(self.allocator, id_copy) catch {\n                        self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n                    };\n                },\n            }\n        }\n\n        stats.failure_ids = failure_ids.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch &.{};\n        return stats;\n    }\n\n    /// Result of applying a single WAL entry.\n    const ApplyResult = enum {\n        applied,\n        skipped,\n        failed,\n    };\n\n    /// Apply a single WAL entry to the store.\n    /// Returns the result of the operation.\n    fn applyEntry(self: *Self, store: *IssueStore, entry: ParsedWalEntry) ApplyResult {\n        _ = self;\n        switch (entry.op) {\n            .add => {\n                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n                    // Only insert if not already present\n                    if (!store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n                        store.insert(issue) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                            error.DuplicateId => return .skipped, // Already exists\n                            else => return .failed,\n                        };\n                        return .applied;\n                    }\n                    return .skipped; // Already exists\n                }\n                return .skipped; // No data for add op\n            },\n            .update => {\n                if (entry.data) |issue| {\n                    // Update or insert\n                    if (store.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n                        // Full replacement for simplicity\n                        const idx = store.id_index.get(issue.id).?;\n                        var old = &store.issues.items[idx];\n                        old.deinit(store.allocator);\n                        store.issues.items[idx] = issue.clone(store.allocator) catch return .failed;\n                        return .applied;\n                    } else {\n                        store.insert(issue) catch return .failed;\n                        return .applied;\n                    }\n                }\n                return .skipped; // No data for update op\n            },\n            .close => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{\n                    .status = .closed,\n                    .closed_at = std.time.timestamp(),\n                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .reopen => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{\n                    .status = .open,\n                }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .delete => {\n                store.delete(entry.id, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .set_blocked => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .blocked }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n            .unset_blocked => {\n                store.update(entry.id, .{ .status = .open }, entry.ts) catch |err| switch (err) {\n                    error.IssueNotFound => return .skipped,\n                    else => return .failed,\n                };\n                return .applied;\n            },\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get the number of entries in the WAL.\n    pub fn entryCount(self: *Self) !usize {\n        const entries = try self.readEntries();\n        defer {\n            for (entries) |*e| {\n                e.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            self.allocator.free(entries);\n        }\n        return entries.len;\n    }\n\n    /// Get the size of the WAL file in bytes.\n    pub fn fileSize(self: *Self) !u64 {\n        const file = fs.cwd().openFile(self.wal_path, .{}) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => return 0,\n            else => return err,\n        };\n        defer file.close();\n\n        const stat = try file.stat();\n        return stat.size;\n    }\n\n    /// Truncate the WAL file (used after compaction).\n    pub fn truncate(self: *Self) !void {\n        const dir = fs.cwd();\n        dir.deleteFile(self.wal_path) catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => {}, // Already empty\n            else => return err,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Convenience methods for common operations\n\n    /// Add a new issue to the WAL.\n    pub fn addIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .add,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = issue.id,\n            .data = issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Close an issue in the WAL.\n    pub fn closeIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .close,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Reopen an issue in the WAL.\n    pub fn reopenIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .reopen,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Update an issue in the WAL.\n    pub fn updateIssue(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .update,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = issue.id,\n            .data = issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Delete an issue in the WAL (tombstone).\n    pub fn deleteIssue(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .delete,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Set an issue as blocked in the WAL.\n    pub fn setBlocked(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .set_blocked,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    /// Unset blocked status in the WAL.\n    pub fn unsetBlocked(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        try self.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .unset_blocked,\n            .ts = std.time.timestamp(),\n            .id = id,\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n};\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"WalOp.toString and fromString roundtrip\" {\n    const ops = [_]WalOp{ .add, .update, .close, .reopen, .delete, .set_blocked, .unset_blocked };\n    for (ops) |op| {\n        const str = op.toString();\n        const parsed = WalOp.fromString(str);\n        try std.testing.expect(parsed != null);\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(op, parsed.?);\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"WalOp.fromString returns null for unknown\" {\n    try std.testing.expect(WalOp.fromString(\"unknown\") == null);\n    try std.testing.expect(WalOp.fromString(\"\") == null);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.init and deinit\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(\".beads\", allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\".beads/beads.wal\", wal.wal_path);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\".beads/beads.lock\", wal.lock_path);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.readEntries  defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    const entries = try wal.readEntries();\n    defer allocator.free(entries);\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), entries.len);\n}\n\ntest \"Wal.appendEntry and readEntries roundtrip\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"wal_roundtrip\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, .id = \"bd-test1\",\n        .data = issue,\n    });\n\n    try wal.appendEntry(.{\n        .op = .close,\n        .ts = 1706540001,\n        .id = \"bd-test1\",\n        .data = null,\n    });\n\n     };\n    69→    }\n    70→\n    71→    /// Get current WAL statistics.\n    72→    pub fn walStats(self: *Self) !WalStats {\n    73→        var wal = try Wal.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n CompactionFailed,\n    WriteError,\n    AtomicRenameFailed,\n    OutOfMemory,\n};\n\n/// Thresholds for automatic compaction.\npub const CompactionThresholds = struct {\n    /// Maximum number of WAL entries before compaction.\n    max_entries: usize = 100,\n    /// Maximum WAL file size in bytes before compaction.\n    max_bytes: u64 = 100 * 1024, // 100KB\n};\n\n/// Statistics about the WAL for monitoring.\npub const WalStats = struct {\n    entry_count: usize,\n    file_size: u64,\n    needs_compaction: bool,\n};\n\n/// Compactor handles WAL compaction operations.\npub const Compactor = struct {\n    beads_dir: []const u8,\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    thresholds: CompactionThresholds,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) Self {\n        return .{\n            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .thresholds = .{},\n        };\n    }\n\n    pub fn initWithThresholds(beads_dir: []const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator, thresholds: CompactionThresholds) Self {\n        return .{\n            .beads_dir = beads_dir,\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .thresholds = thresholds,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Get current WAL statistics.\n    pub fn walStats(self: *Self) !WalStats {\n        var wal = try Wal.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        const entry_count = try wal.entryCount();\n        const file_size = try wal.fileSize();\n\n        return .{\n            .entry_count = entry_count,\n            .file_size = file_size,\n            .needs_compaction = entry_count >= self.thresholds.max_entries or\n                file_size >= self.thresholds.max_bytes,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Trigger compaction if WAL exceeds threshold.\n    /// Returns true if compaction was performed.\n    pub fn maybeCompact(self: *Self) !bool {\n        const stats = try self.walStats();\n        if (stats.needs_compaction) {\n            try self.compact();\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Compact WAL into main file.\n    /// 1. Acquire BeadsLock\n    /// 2. Load beads.jsonl into memory\n    /// 3. Replay beads.wal operations\n    /// 4. Write merged state to beads.jsonl.tmp\n    /// 5. fsync for durability\n    /// 6. Atomic rename over beads.jsonl\n    /// 7. Truncate beads.wal\n    /// 8. Release lock\n    pub fn compact(self: *Self) !void {\n        const lock_path = try std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, \"beads.lock\" });\n        defer self.allocator.free(lock_path);\n\n        const jsonl_path = try std.fs.path.join(self.allocator, &.{ self.beads_dir, \"beads.jsonl\" });\n        defer self.allocator.free(jsonl_path);\n\n        // 1. Acquire exclusive lock\n        var lock = BeadsLock.acquire(lock_path) catch return CompactError.LockFailed;\n        defer lock.release();\n\n        // 2. Load main file into memory\n        var store = IssueStore.init(self.allocator, jsonl_path);\n        defer store.deinit();\n\n        store.loadFromFile() catch |err| switch (err) {\n            error.FileNotFound => {}, // Empty main file is OK\n            else => return CompactError.CompactionFailed,\n        };\n\n        // 3. Replay WAL operations\n        var wal = try Wal.init(self.beads_dir, self.allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        var replay_stats = wal.replay(&store) catch return CompactError.CompactionFailed;\n        defer replay_stats.deinit(self.allocator);\n        // Note: During compaction we proceed even if some replays failed,\n        // since the remaining operations should still be compacted.\n\n        // 4-6. Write merged state atomically\n        try self.writeAtomically(jsonl_path, store.issues.items);\n\n        // 7. Truncate WAL\n        wal.truncate() catch return CompactError.CompactionFailed;\n    }\n\n    /// Write issues to file atomically (temp file + fsync + rename).\n    fn writeAtomically(self: *Self, target_path: []const u8, issues: []const @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue) !void {\n        const dir = fs.cwd();\n\n        // Create temp file path\n        var tmp_path_buf: [std.fs.max_path_bytes]u8 = undefined;\n        const tmp_path = std.fmt.bufPrint(&tmp_path_buf, \"{s}.tmp.{d}\", .{\n            target_path,\n            std.time.milliTimestamp(),\n        }) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n\n        // Write to temp file\n        const tmp_file = dir.createFile(tmp_path, .{}) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n        errdefer {\n            tmp_file.close();\n            dir.deleteFile(tmp_path) catch {};\n        }\n\n        // Serialize and write each issue\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            const json_bytes = std.json.Stringify.valueAlloc(self.allocator, issue, .{}) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n            defer self.allocator.free(json_bytes);\n\n            tmp_file.writeAll(json_bytes) catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n            tmp_file.writeAll(\"\\n\") catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n        }\n\n        // 5. fsync for durability\n        tmp_file.sync() catch return CompactError.WriteError;\n        tmp_file.close();\n\n        // 6. Atomic rename\n        dir.rename(tmp_path, target_path) catch return CompactError.AtomicRenameFailed;\n    }\n\n    /// Force compaction regardless of thresholds.\n    /// Use this for explicit sync operations.\n    pub fn forceCompact(self: *Self) !void {\n        try self.compact();\n    }\n};\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"Compactor.init\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const compactor = Compactor.init(\".beads\", allocator);\n\n    // Verify default thresholds\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 100), compactor.thresholds.max_entries);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 100 * 1024), compactor.thresholds.max_bytes);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.initWithThresholds\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n\n    const compactor = Compactor.initWithThresholds(\".beads\", allocator, .{\n        .max_entries = 50,\n        .max_bytes = 50 * 1024,\n    });\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 50), compactor.thresholds.max_entries);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 50 * 1024), compactor.thresholds.max_bytes);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.walStats returns stats for empty WAL\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_stats_empty\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var compactor = Compactor.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    const stats = try compactor.walStats();\n\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), stats.entry_count);\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u64, 0), stats.file_size);\n    try std.testing.expect(!stats.needs_compaction);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.walStats detects when compaction needed\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_stats_needed\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    // Create WAL with some entries\n    var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    defer wal.deinit();\n\n    const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n    const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-test1\", \"Test Issue\", 1706540000);\n\n    // Add entries up to threshold\n    for (0..5) |i| {\n        try wal.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .add,\n            .ts = 1706540000 + @as(i64, @intCast(i)),\n            .id = \"bd-test1\",\n            .data = issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Test with low threshold\n    var compactor = Compactor.initWithThresholds(test_dir, allocator, .{\n        .max_entries = 3,\n        .max_bytes = 100 * 1024,\n    });\n\n    const stats = try compactor.walStats();\n    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 5), stats.entry_count);\n    try std.testing.expect(stats.needs_compaction);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.maybeCompact skips when below threshold\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_skip\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    var compactor = Compactor.init(test_dir, allocator);\n    const compacted = try compactor.maybeCompact();\n\n    try std.testing.expect(!compacted);\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.compact merges WAL into main file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_merge\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const jsonl_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(jsonl_path);\n\n    const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n\n    // Create initial main file with one issue\n    {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(jsonl_path, allocator);\n        const initial_issues = [_]Issue{\n            Issue.init(\"bd-main1\", \"Main Issue\", 1706540000),\n        };\n        try jsonl.writeAll(&initial_issues);\n    }\n\n    // Add entries to WAL\n    {\n        var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        const new_issue = Issue.init(\"bd-wal1\", \"WAL Issue\", 1706540100);\n        try wal.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .add,\n            .ts = 1706540100,\n            .id = \"bd-wal1\",\n            .data = new_issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Compact\n    {\n        var compactor = Compactor.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        try compactor.compact();\n    }\n\n    // Verify merged result\n    {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(jsonl_path, allocator);\n        const issues = try jsonl.readAll();\n        defer {\n            for (issues) |*issue| {\n                issue.deinit(allocator);\n            }\n            allocator.free(issues);\n        }\n\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 2), issues.len);\n\n        // Check both issues exist (order may vary)\n        var found_main = false;\n        var found_wal = false;\n        for (issues) |issue| {\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.id, \"bd-main1\")) found_main = true;\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, issue.id, \"bd-wal1\")) found_wal = true;\n        }\n        try std.testing.expect(found_main);\n        try std.testing.expect(found_wal);\n    }\n\n    // Verify WAL was truncated\n    {\n        var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        const count = try wal.entryCount();\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 0), count);\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.compact handles close operations\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_close\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const jsonl_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(jsonl_path);\n\n    const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n\n    // Create main file with open issue\n    {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(jsonl_path, allocator);\n        const issues = [_]Issue{\n            Issue.init(\"bd-close1\", \"To Close\", 1706540000),\n        };\n        try jsonl.writeAll(&issues);\n    }\n\n    // Add close operation to WAL\n    {\n        var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        try wal.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .close,\n            .ts = 1706540100,\n            .id = \"bd-close1\",\n            .data = null,\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Compact\n    {\n        var compactor = Compactor.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        try compactor.compact();\n    }\n\n    // Verify issue was closed\n    {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(jsonl_path, allocator);\n        const issues = try jsonl.readAll();\n        defer {\n            for (issues) |*issue| {\n                issue.deinit(allocator);\n            }\n            allocator.free(issues);\n        }\n\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 1), issues.len);\n\n        const Status = @import(\"../models/status.zig\").Status;\n        const issue_status: Status = issues[0].status;\n        try std.testing.expect(issue_status == .closed);\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.compact handles empty main file\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_empty_main\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const jsonl_path = try std.fs.path.join(allocator, &.{ test_dir, \"beads.jsonl\" });\n    defer allocator.free(jsonl_path);\n\n    const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n\n    // Add entry to WAL (no main file)\n    {\n        var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        const issue = Issue.init(\"bd-new1\", \"New Issue\", 1706540000);\n        try wal.appendEntry(.{\n            .op = .add,\n            .ts = 1706540000,\n            .id = \"bd-new1\",\n            .data = issue,\n        });\n    }\n\n    // Compact\n    {\n        var compactor = Compactor.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        try compactor.compact();\n    }\n\n    // Verify main file was created with WAL content\n    {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(jsonl_path, allocator);\n        const issues = try jsonl.readAll();\n        defer {\n            for (issues) |*issue| {\n                issue.deinit(allocator);\n            }\n            allocator.free(issues);\n        }\n\n        try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(usize, 1), issues.len);\n        try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"bd-new1\", issues[0].id);\n    }\n}\n\ntest \"Compactor.maybeCompact triggers at threshold\" {\n    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;\n    const test_dir = try test_util.createTestDir(allocator, \"compact_threshold\");\n    defer allocator.free(test_dir);\n    defer test_util.cleanupTestDir(test_dir);\n\n    const Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\n\n    // Add entries to WAL\n    {\n        var wal = try Wal.init(test_dir, allocator);\n        defer wal.deinit();\n\n        for (0..5) |i| {\n            var id_buf: [32]u8 = undefined;\n            const id = std.fmt.bufPrint(&id_buf, \"bd-test{d}\", .{i}) catch unreachable;\n\n            const issue = Issue.init(id, \"Test Issue\", 1706540000 + @as(i64, @intCast(i)));\n            try wal.appendEntry(.{\n                .op = .add,\n                .ts = 1706540000 + @as(i64, @intCast(i)),\n                .id = id,\n                .data = issue,\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Test with low threshold that should trigger\n    var compactor = Compactor.initWithThresholds(test_dir, allocator, .{\n        .max_entries = 3,\n        .max_bytes = 100 * 1024,\n    });\n\n    const compacted = try compactor.maybeCompact();\n |\n| content_hash | string | no | SHA256 hash for deduplication |\n| title | string | yes | Issue title (1-500 chars) |\n| description | string | no | Detailed description |\n| design | string | no | Design notes |\n| acceptance_criteria | string | no | Definition of done |\n| notes | string | no | Additional notes |\n| status | string | yes | open, in_progress, blocked, deferred, closed, yes | Array of Comment objects |\n\n## WAL Entry (beads.wal)\n\nWrite-ahead log for concurrent writes.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Description |\n|-------|------|-------------|\n| op | string | add, update, close, reopen, delete, set_blocked, unset_blocked |\n| ts | number | Unix timestamp for ordering |\n| id | string | Issue ID |\n| data | object | Full Issue object (for add/update) or null |\n\n## Dependency\n\nEmbedded in Issue.dependencies array.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Description |\n|-------|------|-------------|\n| issue_id | string | Dependent issue |\n| metadata | string | JSON blob for extra data |\n| thread_id | string | Optional thread reference |\n\n## Comment\n\nEmbedded in Issue.comments array.\n\n### Fields\n\n| Field | Type | Description
